<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чиркнуть.html>чи́ркнуть</a> (11609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чиркать.html>чи́ркать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čírkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><b>чи́рк<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:чиркать.html>чи́ркать</a>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čisló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:числить.html>чи́слить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">číslitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to list, to record
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:числить.html>чи́слить</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больны́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>číslitʹ</b> kovó-libo bolʹným</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put on the sick list, to record as sick</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to consider (+ instrumental, as)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to count, to calculate</li></ol>

***чистить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a> (4379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čistiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čístitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почистить.html>почи́стить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clean, to scour</li>
<li>to peel</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čísto</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-чи́сто" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чи́ще</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cleanly, neatly</li>
<li>purely, merely</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čísto</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>чис<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>сер</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>де́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистота.html>чистота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čistotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистота.html>чистоты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

***чистый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a> (595)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čistъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čístyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чи́ще</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clean, tidy</li>
<li>clean, clear, pure</li></ol>

***читать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> (301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čitati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочитать.html>прочита́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почитать.html>почита́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прочесть.html>проче́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to read
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> pro sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read silently, to read to oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:строка.html>стро́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> méždu strók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read between the lines</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запинка.html>запи́нки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> bez zapínki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read off, to run off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запеть.html>запо́ем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> zapójem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read avidly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> mýsli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read minds</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вслух.html>вслух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> vslux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read aloud</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́тся</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne znájet, a <b>čitátʹ</b> sadítsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">learn to speak before you sing</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">he/she doesn’t know but to sit for reading</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́й</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропускать.html>пропуска́й</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne vsjó <b>čitáj</b>, inóje propuskáj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">do not read everything (aloud), skip some</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́й</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разуметь.html>разуме́й</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne mnógo <b>čitáj</b>, da mnógo razuméj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no need to read a lot, but to understand a lot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to recite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наизусть.html>наизу́сть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> naizústʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to recite by heart</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lecture, to give a lecture, to deliver a lecture
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лекция.html>ле́кции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> lékcii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lecture</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to teach
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:курс.html>курс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> kurs</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give a course</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tell, to say (for the purpose of a lesson)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нотация.html>нота́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> notácii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jaw</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> morálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to moralize</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pronounce, to deliver
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молитва.html>моли́твы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> molítvy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to say one’s prayers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проповедь.html>про́поведь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> própovedʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to preach</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> рэп</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> rɛp</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to flow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand, to interpret, to decipher
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чертеж.html>чертежи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> čerteží</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to interpret drawings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čitátʹ</b> kártu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read a map</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:прочитать.html>прочита́ть</a>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читаться.html>чита́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čitátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прочита́ться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почитаться.html>почита́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проче́сться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to read
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:легко.html>легко́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:читаться.html>чита́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kníga lexkó <b>čitájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this book reads easily</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel like reading
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> что́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:читаться.html>чита́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú štó-to ne <b>čitájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he doesn't feel like reading; he is not in the right mood for reading</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***читающий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:читающий.html>чита́ющий</a> (301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читающий.html>чита́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čitájuščij</span>)

***чихать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чихать.html>чиха́ть</a> (11965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čixati</i>, of onomatopoeic origin. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">чи́хамь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">číhamʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Gerov), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">číhati</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">čȋham</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">čichać</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">tśichaś</i>. Also found as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чхать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьxati</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чха́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čxáty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">чхаць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čxacʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">czchać</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чихать.html>чиха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čixátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чихнуть.html>чихну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sneeze</li>
<li>to scorn, to disdain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чихать.html>чиха́ть</a></b> <i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>)</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>čixátʹ</b> <i>(na)</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't give a damn <i>(for)</i>, I don't care a button <i>(about)</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ха́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
<a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:чихнуть.html>чихну́ть</a> (знач. 1, 2); начихать, <a href = vnd.unilang:начхать.html>начха́ть</a> (знач. 3).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-чих-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
